from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
html_doc = """
<html><head><title>Chang's Web Site</title></head>
<body>
<p class="title"><b>張恩睿</b></p>

<p class="story">張恩睿出生在台北，父親
<a href="http://example.com/parentsf" class="Ancestor" id="link1">張錫隆</a>
母親
<a href="http://example.com/parentsm" class="Ancestor" id="link2">林寶絲</a>
在台灣台北出生，</p>
<p class="story">...</p>
</html>
"""

chang = BeautifulSoup(html_doc, 'html.parser')
# BeautifulSoup回傳的值(Chiang)是一個有巢狀(nested)的資料結構。
print(chang.prettify())

<script type="text/javascript" id="getPageParams">
    var messagingClient = window.messagingClient || MessagingClient.instantiate();

    var onErrorParams = function (url, error) {
        var message = messagingClient.create('log',
            {
                level: 'error',
                message: '[HomePageParams]:' + url + ':' + error,
                applicationName: 'www.agoda.com'
            });
        messagingClient.send(message);
    };

    agoda = window.agoda || {};
    agoda.perf = {};
    agoda.perf.getData = function (url) {
        return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
            var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.onreadystatechange = function () {
                if (xhr.readyState == XMLHttpRequest.DONE) {
                    try {
                        var result = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
                        resolve(result);
                    } catch (ex) {
                        onErrorParams(url, "Error parsing from JSON: " + ex);
                        reject("Error parsing from JSON: " + ex);
                    }
                }
            };

            xhr.onerror = function (err) {
                onErrorParams(url, "Error getting response:" + err);

                reject("Error getting response: " + xhr.status);
            };

            xhr.open('GET', url, true);
            xhr.send(null);
        })
    };

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    function areCookiesEnabled() {
        try {
            document.cookie = 'test_cookie_enabled=1';
            var ret = document.cookie.indexOf('test_cookie_enabled=') !== -1;
            document.cookie = 'test_cookie_enabled=1; expires=Thu, 01-Jan-1970 00:00:01 GMT';
            return ret;
        }
        catch (e) {
            return false;
        }
    }

    if (!areCookiesEnabled()) {
        document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', "\u003cdiv class=\"CookieWarning\"\u003e \u003cdiv class=\"CookieWarning__center\"\u003e \u003cdiv class=\"CookieWarning__container\"\u003e \u003cp class=\"CookieWarning__title\"\u003e需允許Cookies存取\u003c/p\u003e \u003cp\u003e你的瀏覽器目前設定為不允取存取Cookies，請允取Cookies存取才能繼續。\u003c/p\u003e \u003c/div\u003e \u003c/div\u003e \u003c/div\u003e");
    }

<script>
        (function(defaultTileTheme) {
            var tileContainer = document.getElementById('TileContainer');
            if (!tileContainer) return;
            if (window.location.hash.indexOf('homes') >= 0)
            {
                tileContainer.className = 'TileContainer TileContainer--homes';
            }
            else if ( 
                (false && window.location.hash.indexOf('#homes') === -1 && window.location.hash.indexOf('#rooms') ===-1 ) 
                    || window.location.hash.indexOf('#flights') >= 0) {
                tileContainer.className = 'TileContainer TileContainer--full TileContainer--flights';
            }
            else
            {
                tileContainer.className = 'TileContainer TileContainer--' + defaultTileTheme;
            }
        })('orange');
</script>

function getUrlVars() {\r\n            var vars = [], hash;\r\n            var hashes = window.location.href.slice(window.location.href.indexOf(\'?\') + 1).split(\'&\');\r\n            for (var i = 0; i < hashes.length; i++) {\r\n                hash = hashes[i].split(\'=\');\r\n                vars.push(hash[0]);\r\n                vars[hash[0]] = hash[1];\r\n            }\r\n            return vars;\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        function getBreakPointType_5types(width) {\r\n            if (width < 480) {\r\n                return "phone"\r\n            } else if (width >= 480 && width < 600) {\r\n                return "tablet"\r\n            } else if (width >= 600 && width < 940) {\r\n                return "default600"\r\n            } else if (width >= 940 && width < 1170) {\r\n                return "default940"\r\n            } else {\r\n                //return "default1170"\r\n                return "default"\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        //最近一個營業日不可比較幣別，比較幣別為空時不顯示現金&即期\r\n        function search_range_check(search_range) {\r\n            if (search_range.val() == \'ltm\' || search_range.val() == \'month\' || search_range.val() == \'l6m\' || search_range.val() == \'l1y\' || search_range.val() == \'l3y\') {\r\n                $(\'select[name=compare]\').prop(\'disabled\', false);\r\n                if ($(\'select[name=compare]\').val()) { $(\'#datatype\').show(); } else {\r\n                    $(\'#datatype\').hide();\r\n                }\r\n            } else {\r\n }\r\n\r\n        //去footable上面多的線&下面多的線\r\n        function footableHideNodataBottom() {\r\n            $(".footable-row-detail-row").each(function () {\r\n                if ($(this).find("div.footable-row-detail-name").html() == "") {\r\n                    $(this).hide();\r\n                }\r\n            })\r\n            $(".footable-row-detail-row:last-child").css("border-bottom", "0px #ddd solid");\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        //去除url中lang參數\r\n        function removeUrlLang(urlSearch) {\r\n            urlSearch = urlSearch.replace("?Lang=zh-TW&", "").replace("?Lang=en-US&", "").replace("?Lang=zh-CN&", "");\r\n            urlSearch = urlSearch.replace("?Lang=zh-TW", "").replace("?Lang=en-US", "").replace("?Lang=zh-CN", "").replace("?Lang=ja-JP", "");\r\n\r\n            urlSearch = urlSearch.replace("?lang=zh-TW&", "").replace("?lang=en-US&", "").replace("?lang=zh-CN&", "");\r\n            urlSearch = urlSearch.replace("?lang=zh-TW", "").replace("?lang=en-US", "").replace("?lang=zh-CN", "");\r\n\r\n            urlSearch = urlSearch.replace("?", "");\r\n            if (urlSearch != "") {\r\n                return "&" + urlSearch;\r\n            } else {\r\n                return urlSearch;\r\n            }\r\n        }\r\n\r\n        //觸發多語系連結\r\n        function ChangeLanguage(lang) {\r\n            switch (lang) {\r\n                case "zh-TW" || "zh-tw":\r\n                    if (location.search == "") {\r\n                        window.location.href = encodeURI(location.pathname) + "?Lang=zh-TW";\r\n                    } else {\r\n                        window.location.href = encodeURI(location.pathname) + "?Lang=zh-TW" + removeUrlLang(location.search);\r\n                    }\r\n                    break;\r\n                case "zh-CN" || "zh-cn":\r\n                    if (location.search == "") {\r\n                        window.location.href = encodeURI(location.pathname) + "?Lang=zh-CN";\r\n                    } else {\r\n                        window.location.href = encodeURI(location.pathname) + "?Lang=zh-CN" + removeUrlLang(location.search);\r\n                    }\r\n                    break;\r\n                case "en-US" || "en-us":\r\n                    if (location.search == "") {\r\n                        window.location.href = encodeURI(location.pathname) + "?Lang=en-US";\r\n                    } else {\r\n                        window.location.href = encodeURI(location.pathname) + "?Lang=en-US" + removeUrlLang(location.search);\r\n                    }\r\n                    break;\r\n                case "ja-JP" || "ja-jp":\r\n                    if (location.search == "") {\r\n                        window.location.href = encodeURI(location.pathname) + "?Lang=ja-JP";\r\n                    } else {\r\n
